4306:docs/phase3-prep-slice-plan.md:74:- **Pipeline schema extension — header-aware v2 adapter, v1 path untouched (Codex P1 + round-1 #5):** `read_source()` currently **drops headers** and `normalize_row()` uses **positional indexes** with hardcoded valid emails / `opt_in = "unknown"` / blank suppression ([scripts/pipeline.py:268](../scripts/pipeline.py:268)) — so a naive "read more columns" extension is brittle (column order would silently matter).
